# Quest Hub Expansion — Emberwild_DepthPack_GIGA_Part2_2025-12-24_QuestHub_Expansion

1500 grounded quests (QST-2000 → QST-3499).

## QST-2000 — Chalk on the Third Plank (Frostbriar)
- **Giver:** Lantern Keeper
- **Type:** Craft
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Emberford Tea** (ID 40770).
  2. Collect **Tide-taken Belt** (ID 40256) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Glimmerdeep Ration** (ID 41643) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Lantern-lit Permit Slip** (ID 42054) *or* **Harbor-wet Cloak** (ID 40173)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.

- **Type:** Escort
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Mire-touched Ration** (ID 41845).
  2. Collect **Silt-grit Cloak** (ID 40793) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Storm-bit Root** (ID 40348) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Storm-bit Vest** (ID 40152) *or* **Moon-stitched Canteen** (ID 40568)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.

- **Type:** Craft
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Saltmarrow Keybone** (ID 44839).
  2. Collect **Mire-touched Lantern** (ID 44070) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Silt-grit Trophy Fang** (ID 41090) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Frostbriar Hood** (ID 41341) *or* **Amberwake Bottle** (ID 41654)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.

- **Type:** Deliver
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Frostbriar Bandage Roll** (ID 42880).
  2. Collect **Silt-grit Keybone** (ID 44721) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Deliver **Hollowroot Leather Strip** (ID 41495) to a local contact.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Storm-bit Canteen** (ID 43187) *or* **Mire-touched Lantern** (ID 43396)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.
